class="framer-q9ch8x" data-framer-name="inner-hero" name="inner-hero"><div class="framer-1fcebz7" data-framer-name="Container" name="Container"><div class="framer-198cr39"><div class="framer-tcpy73" style="--framer-text-alignment:center;--framer-text-color:var(--token-e357fef8-33e6-40aa-b2ac-a7ef2da90600, rgb(88, 105, 252))">Last Updated: January 22, 2024</p></div><div class="framer-smhpwl" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><h1 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-133jal" data-styles-preset="XEK23sgrB" style="--framer-text-alignment:center;--framer-text-color:var(--token-7f5544af-543d-45ce-a4d1-c4fb6f3243f4, rgb(24, 28, 57))">Privacy Policy for DocGPT</h1></div></div></div></div></header><div class="framer-1ilwz25" data-framer-name="Privacy" name="Privacy"><div class="framer-xgi6x" data-framer-name="Container" name="Container"><div class="framer-7bi7yn" data-framer-name="row" name="row"><header class="framer-1wnum2u" data-framer-name="content" name="content"><div class="framer-1n8eevf" data-framer-name="List-01" name="List-01"><div class="framer-ekkh9j" data-framer-name="title" name="title"><div class="framer-1es5jqg" data-framer-name="heading" name="heading"><div class="framer-9dr19t" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">Introduction</p></div></div><div class="framer-tw7cn6" data-framer-name="Paragraph" name="Paragraph"><div class="framer-q9jd4f" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">Privacy is at the heart of everything we do at eesel. Our extension is <a class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1lodeke" data-styles-preset="XhaIpOzcJ" href="https://www.fastcompany.com/90766562/the-23-best-new-productivity-apps-for-2022" rel="noopener">Fast Company&#x2019;s best new apps</a> and has 11k monthly users in companies like Atlassian, Shopify and Intercom. A key reason for our success has been our privacy first approach.<br class="framer-text"><br class="framer-text trailing-break"></p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">We&#x2019;re now kicking off GPTs like Docs GPT. You&#x2019;ll be able to ask any question to the app and it will answer based on your company knowledge like your Google Docs. Here&#x2019;s a run through privacy related questions related to this. </p></div></div></div></div><div class="framer-1bbrrf9" data-framer-name="List-02" name="List-02"><div class="framer-9ghfj5" data-framer-name="title" name="title"><div class="framer-1fnqwkm" data-framer-name="heading" name="heading"><div class="framer-1jf2mht" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">How is data accessed?</p></div></div><div class="framer-1vkdiz0" data-framer-name="Paragraph" name="Paragraph"><div class="framer-157vp5n" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">You have full control over what data is made available to the app. The app will read page data you give access to when you sign in via Google OAuth. We use the drive.file scope, which means that you will be able to pick exactly which pages you give access to. In addition, user profile data like name and email is requested to create an account and authorise you with eesel.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="framer-r0q5ar" data-framer-name="List-03" name="List-03"><div class="framer-gkcubs" data-framer-name="title" name="title"><div class="framer-1bozuqu" data-framer-name="heading" name="heading"><div class="framer-12vb4uw" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">How is the data used?</p></div></div><div class="framer-10ei771" data-framer-name="Paragraph" name="Paragraph"><div class="framer-mrvvi3" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">When a question is asked to the app, the page data is the context the GPT bases the responses on. Specifically, when you ask a question, eesel finds relevant Google Docs, Slides, Sheets that are relevant to that question, and then passes this on as context for your ChatGPT, and then crafts a response for you. The app is only an observer of the data you explicitly grant access to, ensuring privacy and control over your data. </p></div></div></div></div><div class="framer-xfp61l" data-framer-name="title" name="title"><div class="framer-1iy1wf6" data-framer-name="heading" name="heading"><div class="framer-i51g2s" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">How is the data stored?</p></div></div><div class="framer-mvajed" data-framer-name="Paragraph" name="Paragraph"><div class="framer-1np3xi3" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">The data you provide access to is securely stored in a SOC2 Type II certified vector database in the form of embeddings (mathematical representations). These embeddings are crucial for the app to answer questions. When a request is made, the app uses the embeddings to find related pages and conversations, and shares only specific relevant snippets with <a class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-aexbeb" data-styles-preset="stylesPresetLink" href="https://openai.com/" rel="noopener">OpenAI</a> to generate the response.</p></div></div></div><div class="framer-wt3mw0" data-framer-name="List-04" name="List-04"><div class="framer-bjdn9v" data-framer-name="title" name="title"><div class="framer-1hqnbpt" data-framer-name="heading" name="heading"><div class="framer-1cf5ss7" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">How long is the data retained?</p></div></div><div class="framer-68avi7" data-framer-name="Paragraph" name="Paragraph"><div class="framer-1d79eai" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">Data is retained throughout the subscription period and for an additional 30 days after subscription termination. After this period, all associated data is permanently deleted. Data shared with OpenAI is retained for abuse and misuse monitoring for a maximum of 30 days, and then it is deleted.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="framer-l1u54u" data-framer-name="title" name="title"><div class="framer-16o4m7y" data-framer-name="heading" name="heading"><div class="framer-1kqwoga" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">Is Google user data used or shared?</p></div></div><div class="framer-152nlzd" data-framer-name="Paragraph" name="Paragraph"><div class="framer-17txexw" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">Google user data like name and email is never shared with any party. It&apos;s only used to authenticate and associate your account. Likewise, any access to your page data you provide (like your Google Docs, Slides or Sheets) is never shared with anyone. It is stored in your dedicated database, only for you to chat with.</p></div></div></div><div class="framer-77ya81" data-framer-name="List-05" name="List-05"><div class="framer-1lx4zkg" data-framer-name="title" name="title"><div class="framer-6id9ah" data-framer-name="heading" name="heading"><div class="framer-1cji0sm" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">What security measures have been implemented?</p></div></div><div class="framer-1gnbkp5" data-framer-name="Paragraph" name="Paragraph"><div class="framer-1j9icr5" data-framer-name="text box" name="text box"><div class="framer-1y6hnvw" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">Security is a top priority for us and we have implemented various best practices to ensure data protection. Here are some key measures:</p><ol class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Secure Data storage: We use Pinecone, a SOC2 Type II certified vector database, to store data securely. Our system uses a multi-tenant architecture, ensuring that customer data is isolated from one another.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Encryption and Network Security: We follow several best practices like using Transport Layer Security (TLS) to encrypt all traffic. Network security measures, including firewalls, are implemented to protect against unauthorized access.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Access Controls and Data Handling: Access control is enforced through Identity and Access Management (IAM) mechanisms, ensuring that only authorized personnel can access sensitive data. We have 2FA on all sensitive tools, and handle client ID, secret, and bot tokens with utmost care.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Least Privilege Principle: We only request the necessary scopes and &quot;least privilege&quot; tokens required for the app&apos;s functionality. For example, we request messaging access only for Slack channels the bot is explicitly added to, which is crucial for the app to function.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Role-Based Access Control (RBAC): By default, only the admin user, who initially installed the app, has access to configure the app (like add more pages on which the responses are based). We have RBAC mechanisms that allow the admin to grant explicit access permissions to authorized personnel. This ensures that only individuals with the necessary authorization can configure the app.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Security Audits and Penetration Testing: We regularly perform security audits and penetration testing to identify and address any potential vulnerabilities promptly. We can provide a summary of the last internal penetration report on request.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Supplier Management: We conduct risk assessments of suppliers in accordance with our <a class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-aexbeb" data-styles-preset="stylesPresetLink" href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1JIJOFWBTA4atMNWi20nUoAIO2VC30OPudjMGjWOTNFw/edit" rel="noopener">supplier management policy</a>.</p></li></ol><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">We understand that you trust us with your data when you use our app, and we don&apos;t take that trust lightly. Feel free to reach out for any clarifications and additional questions.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="framer-10mmc3u" data-framer-name="List-06" name="List-06"><div class="framer-fo1d0u" data-framer-name="title" name="title"><div class="framer-167xrhi" data-framer-name="heading" name="heading"><div class="framer-bqwol9" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">What does Open AI / ChatGPT do with the data shared?</p></div></div><div class="framer-fsgnfn" data-framer-name="Paragraph" name="Paragraph"><div class="framer-1lv6750" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">OpenAI does not use data submitted to train or improve their models. Any data sent is retained for abuse and misuse monitoring purposes for a maximum of 30 days, after which it is deleted. You can <a class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-aexbeb" data-styles-preset="stylesPresetLink" href="https://openai.com/policies/api-data-usage-policies" rel="noopener">read more here</a>.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="framer-19n4mhh" data-framer-name="List-07" name="List-07"><div class="framer-ijb8kx" data-framer-name="title" name="title"><div class="framer-2hwora" data-framer-name="heading" name="heading"><div class="framer-hoe252" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">What subprocessors do you use?</p></div></div><div class="framer-1mmzjcu" data-framer-name="Paragraph" name="Paragraph"><div class="framer-7cm1d9" style="outline:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;justify-content:flex-start;flex-shrink:0;transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-1syiuv7" data-styles-preset="NaJHE7gVf">Here is a full list of sub processors:&#x200b;&#x200b; <a class="framer-text" href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/18ja94HSiZPIaOypZVhDO2raYEtFNIXSXjQYInjzncTE" rel="noopener">eesel Subprocessor list</a>. OpenAI is the key service we use to power eesel AI.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="framer-2401aa" data-framer-name="List-07" name="List-07"><div class="framer-1yevtuh" data-framer-name="title" framer-styles-preset-oa5aox" data-styles-preset="fbPY4mLua">How can I request access, transfer, or deletion of my data?</p></div></div><div class="framer-fy3vc0" data-framer-name="Paragraph"
